about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> Behavioral methods to\
  \ study cognitive development in infants, probing infants\u2019 evolving understanding\
  \ of objects and their physical behaviors, and understanding of agents who engage\
  \ in goal-directed activity and initiate social interactions.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong>\
  \ Liz Spelke</p>"

  <span m='1777290'>ideal</span> <span m='1777800'>medium</span> <span m='1778280'>for</span>

  <span m='1780770'>new</span> <span m='1781040'>concepts.</span> </p><p><span m='1782790'>One</span>
  <span m='1783410'>is</span> <span m='1783710'>that</span> <span m='1784310'>the</span>

  <span m='1785330'>rules</span> <span m='1786020'>of--</span> <span m='1786560'>well,</span>
  <span m='1786710'>three</span> <span m='1786920'>properties,</span> <span m='1787370'>actually.</span>
  <span m='1788090'>One</span> <span m='1788360'>is</span> <span m='1788480'>that</span>

  <span m='1795300'>That</span> <span m='1795470'>is,</span> <span m='1796370'>if</span>
